<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">explosion</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">explōsiōnis</i>, genitive form of <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">explōsio</i>, from <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">explōdo</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">I drive out by clapping</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">ex-</i> and <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">plōdo</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">I clap or strike</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

***extremiteit.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:extremiteit.html>extremiteit</a> (131256)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <small>[Term?]</small> (recorded circa 1265), from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_French" class="extiw" title="w:Old French">Old French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro">extrémité</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">extremitas</i>. Equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:extreem.html>extreem</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-iteit</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:extremiteit.html>extremiteit</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:extremiteiten.html>extremiteiten</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:extremiteit.html>extremiteitje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>An extremity (ulterior point or side)</li>
<li>A bodily extremity, member, limb</li>
<li>An extreme peril</li>
<li>An ultimate or decisive battle</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:uiterste.html>uiterste</a></span> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span></li>
<li>(limb) <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ledemaat.html>ledemaat</a></span></li>
<li>(ultimate battle) <span class="Latn" lang="nl">eindstrijd</span> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span></li></ul>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related <a href = vnd.unilang:terms.html>terms</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:ezel.html>ezel</a> (4306)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">ēsel</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">esil</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-West_Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-West Germanic language">Proto-West Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gmw-pro">*asil</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Late_Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Late Latin">Late Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">asellus</i>.<sup id="cite_ref-1" class="reference"><a href="cite_note-1"> | 1 | </a></sup>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ezel.html>ezel</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ezels.html>ezels</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ezeltje.html>ezeltje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>donkey, ass
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>Een</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:ezel.html>ezel</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:balkt.html>balkt</a>: “i-aa, i-aa”.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">A <b>donkey</b> howls: “ee-aa, ee-aa”.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>fool, idiot

Dumb <b>asses</b>!</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>easel
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:ezel.html>Ezel</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:en.html>en</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:palet.html>palet</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:zijn.html>zijn</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:onmisbaar.html>onmisbare</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:hulpmiddelen.html>hulpmiddelen</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> landschapsschilder.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation"><b>Easel</b> and palette are essential tools of the landscape painter.</span></dd></dl></div></dd>

***ezelsoor.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:ezelsoor.html>ezelsoor</a> (106962)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ezel.html>ezel</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">donkey, ass</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-s-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="ann-pos">genitive interfix</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:oor.html>oor</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">ear; handle</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. The sense “dog-ear” <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> a calque of  <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Eselsohr</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ezelsoor.html>ezelsoor</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ezelsoren.html>ezelsoren</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ezelsoor.html>ezelsoortje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>donkey's ear</li>

<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_French" class="extiw" title="w:Middle French">Middle French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="frm">faction</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">factiō</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">a group of people acting together, a political faction</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, noun of process from <a href = vnd.unilang:perfect.html>perfect</a> passive participle <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">factus</i>, from <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">faciō</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">do, make</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_French" class="extiw" title="w:Old French">Old French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro">faculté</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">facultas</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">capability, ability, skill, abundance, plenty, stock, goods, properly</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Medieval_Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Medieval Latin">Medieval Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">facultas</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">a body of teachers</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, another form of <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">facilitas</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">easiness, facility, etc.</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">facul</i>, another form of <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">facilis</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">easy, facile</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. See <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">facile</i>.
</p>

***fagot.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:fagot.html>fagot</a> (51978)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_5">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Italian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Italian language">Italian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="it">fagotto</i>. <a href = vnd.unilang:later.html>Later</a> borrowed again from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Fagott</i>. The theory that the name derives from a faggot of stick in reference to the way the parts of a bassoon are stored <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> a pseudo-etymology. <sup id="cite_ref-1" class="reference"><a href="cite_note-1"> | 1 | </a></sup>
</p>

</p>
<ol><li>bassoon</li></ol>

***faillissement.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:faillissement.html>faillissement</a> (27179)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From earlier <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">faillement</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_French" class="extiw" title="w:Middle French">Middle French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="frm">faillement</i>, from <i class="Latn mention" lang="frm">faillir</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to fail, go bankrupt</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. The insertion of <i>-iss-</i> happened in Dutch as a hyperforeignism, and <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> not found in the French word.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:faillissement.html>faillissement</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:faillissementen.html>faillissementen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:faillissement.html>faillissementje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">law</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A bankruptcy.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">figuratively</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> The demise, the undoing of something or someone.</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">legal</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span><span class="ib-colon sense-qualifier-colon">:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl">achteruitvaart</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:bankroet.html>bankroet</a></span>, <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:failliet.html>failliet</a></span>, <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:faling.html>faling</a></span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">demise</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span><span class="ib-colon sense-qualifier-colon">:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:failliet.html>failliet</a></span>, <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ondergang.html>ondergang</a></span>, <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:einde.html>einde</a></span></li></ul>

***fain.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:fain.html>fain</a> (65213)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_English" class="extiw" title="w:Middle English">Middle English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm"><a href = vnd.unilang:fain.html>fain</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_English" class="extiw" title="w:Old English">Old English</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ang">fægen</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*faganaz</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">glad</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*peḱ-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to make pretty, please oneself</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>; akin to <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Norse" class="extiw" title="w:Old Norse">Old <a href = vnd.unilang:norse.html>Norse</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="non">feginn</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">glad, joyful</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Gothic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Gothic language">Gothic</a></span> <i class="Goth mention" lang="got">𐍆𐌰𐌲𐌹𐌽𐍉𐌽</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="got-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">faginōn</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to rejoice</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Norse" class="extiw" title="w:Old Norse">Old <a href = vnd.unilang:norse.html>Norse</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="non">fagna</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to rejoice</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.<sup id="cite_ref-1" class="reference"><a href="cite_note-1"> | 1 | </a></sup>
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:fain.html>fain</a></strong> (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en comparative-form-of" lang="en">more <a href = vnd.unilang:fain.html>fain</a></b>, <i>superlative</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en superlative-form-of" lang="en">most <a href = vnd.unilang:fain.html>fain</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">archaic</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> Well-pleased, glad.
<ul><li><b>1485</b>, <a href = vnd.unilang:sir.html>Sir</a> <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Thomas_Malory" class="extiw" title="w:Thomas Malory">Thomas Malory</a>, <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://quod.lib.umich.edu/c/cme/MaloryWks2/1:19.1?rgn=div2;view=fulltext">chapter primum</a>, in <i><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Le_Morte_d%27Arthur" class="extiw" title="w:Le Morte d | Arthur">Le <a href = vnd.unilang:morte.html>Morte</a> Darthur</a></i>, book XVII:
<dl><dd>Thus Gawayne and Ector abode to gyder / For syre Ector wold not awey <a href = vnd.unilang:til.html>til</a> Gawayne <a href = vnd.unilang:were.html>were</a> hole / amp; the good knyȝt Galahad <a href = vnd.unilang:rode.html>rode</a> so long tyll he <a href = vnd.unilang:came.html>came</a> that nyghte to the <a href = vnd.unilang:castel.html>Castel</a> of Carboneck / amp; hit befelle hym thus / that he <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> benyghted in an hermytage / <a href = vnd.unilang:soo.html>Soo</a> the good <a href = vnd.unilang:man.html>man</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> <b>fayne</b> whan he sawe he <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> a knyght erraunt</dd></dl></li></ul></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">archaic</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> Satisfied, contented.
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1883</b>,  <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Dante_Gabriel_Rossetti" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Dante Gabriel Rossetti"><a href = vnd.unilang:dante.html>Dante</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:gabriel.html>Gabriel</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:rossetti.html>Rossetti</a></a>, <i>A Death-Parting</i>, line 11,  <cite><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://books.google.com/books?id=KmQFAAAAQAAJamp;pg=PA285amp;lpg=PA285">Poems</a></cite>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:o.html>O</a> love, of my death my life <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:fain.html>fain</a></b>,</span></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">archaic</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> Eager, willing or inclined to.
<ul><li><i>c.</i> <b>1591</b>, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/William_Shakespeare" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:William Shakespeare">William Shakespeare</a>, <i><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Henry_VI,_Part_2" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Henry VI, Part 2"><a href = vnd.unilang:henry.html>Henry</a> VI, Part 2</a></i>, Act II scene i<sup><a rel="nofollow" class="external autonumber" href="http://shakespeare.mit.edu/Shakespeare/2henryvi/">[1]</a></sup>:
<dl><dd><a href = vnd.unilang:men.html>Men</a> and <a href = vnd.unilang:birds.html>birds</a> are <b><a href = vnd.unilang:fain.html>fain</a></b> of climbing high.</dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="maintenance-line" style="color: 777777;">(Can <a href = vnd.unilang:we.html>we</a> date this quote by Jeremy <a href = vnd.unilang:taylor.html>Taylor</a> and provide title, author’s full name, and other <a href = vnd.unilang:details.html>details</a>?)</span>
<dl><dd>To a busy <a href = vnd.unilang:man.html>man</a>, temptation <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:fain.html>fain</a></b> to climb up together with his business.</dd></dl></li></ul></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">archaic</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> Obliged or compelled to.</li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_English" class="extiw" title="w:Middle English">Middle English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm"><a href = vnd.unilang:fain.html>fain</a></i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm">fayn</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm">feyn</i>, from the adjective (see above).
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Adverb">Adverb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:fain.html>fain</a></strong> (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en comparative-form-of" lang="en">fainer</b>, <i>superlative</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en superlative-form-of" lang="en">fainest</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">archaic</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> With joy; gladly.
<ul><li><i>c.</i> <b>1598-99</b>, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/William_Shakespeare" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:William Shakespeare">William Shakespeare</a>, <i><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Much_Ado_About_Nothing" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Much Ado About Nothing">Much Ado About Nothing</a></i>, Act III scene v<sup><a rel="nofollow" class="external autonumber" href="http://www.opensourceshakespeare.org/views/plays/playmenu.php?WorkID=muchado">[2]</a></sup>:
<dl><dd><span style="font-variant:small-caps;">Leonato</span>: I would <b><a href = vnd.unilang:fain.html>fain</a></b> know what you have to say.</dd></dl></li>
<li><b>1633</b>, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/John_Donne" class="extiw" title="w:John Donne">John Donne</a>, <i><a href="https://en.wikisource.org/wiki/Holy_Sonnets" class="extiw" title="s:Holy Sonnets"><a href = vnd.unilang:holly.html>Holly</a> Sonnets</a></i>, XIV:
<dl><dd>Yet dearly I love you, and would be <a href = vnd.unilang:loved.html>loved</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:fain.html>fain</a></b>, / But am betroth’d unto your enemy</dd></dl></li>
<li><b>1719</b>, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Daniel_Defoe" class="extiw" title="w:Daniel Defoe"><a href = vnd.unilang:daniel.html>Daniel</a> Defoe</a>, <i><a href="https://en.wikisource.org/wiki/Robinson_Crusoe" class="extiw" title="s:Robinson Crusoe">Robinson Crusoe</a></i>:
<dl><dd>The second thing I <b><a href = vnd.unilang:fain.html>fain</a></b> would have <a href = vnd.unilang:had.html>had</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> a tobacco-pipe, but it <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> impossible to <a href = vnd.unilang:me.html>me</a> to make one…</dd></dl></li></ul></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">archaic</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> By will or choice.
<ul><li><i>c.</i> <b>1610-11</b>, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/William_Shakespeare" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:William Shakespeare">William Shakespeare</a>, <i><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/The_Tempest" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:The Tempest">The Tempest</a></i>, Act I scene i<sup><a rel="nofollow" class="external autonumber" href="http://www.opensourceshakespeare.org/views/plays/play_view.php?WorkID=tempestamp;Scope=entireamp;pleasewait=1amp;msg=pl">[3]</a></sup>:
<dl><dd><span style="font-variant:small-caps;">Gonzalo</span>:  Now would I give a thousand furlongs of sea for an acre of barren ground— long heath, brown furze, anything. The wills above be done, but I would <b><a href = vnd.unilang:fain.html>fain</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:die.html>die</a> a dry death.</dd></dl></li></ul></li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_3">Etymology 3</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_English" class="extiw" title="w:Middle English">Middle English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm">fainen</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_English" class="extiw" title="w:Old English">Old English</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ang">fæġenian</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-West_Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-West Germanic language">Proto-West Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gmw-pro">*faginōn</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*faginōną</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:fain.html>fain</a></strong> (<i>third-person singular simple present</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en 3 | s | pres-form-of" lang="en">fains</b>, <i>present participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en pres | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">faining</b>, <i>simple past and past participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en past | and | past | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">fained</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">archaic</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> To be delighted or glad; to rejoice.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">archaic</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> To gladden.</li></ol>
</body>
